 bharat main saamaajik or aarthik asamanta ko ujagar karti ‘institute of objective studies' kii taaja report ke anusaar tamaam muslim bahul siton kaa anusuchit jatiyon ke liye arakshit hona muslim pratinidhitiv kii raah main baadhak he

 iske baavjood 20 pratishat se adhik muslim aabaadi vaali nau siten anusuchit jati evam janajati ke liye arakshit hone ke kaaran in par muslim pratinidhitiv ke daravaaje band ho gayi
